***анафема.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a> (27756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνάθεμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anáthema</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anáfema</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фемы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фемы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фем</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anathema, excommunication</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scolding word
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">макси́м <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Maksím Górʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  <cite><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Tróje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></cite>  | <cite>The Three</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Лунёв <a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ненавидеть.html>ненави́дя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мал</a>: «<a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>Хоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывихнуть.html>вы́вихнула</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a>...»</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lunjóv molčál i, nenavídja jejó vsej dušój, dúmal: “Xotʹ by ty, <b>anáfema</b>, nógu sebé vývixnula, prýgaja tut...”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Lunyov was silent and, hating her with his whole heart, thought: "<b>Anathema</b>, I wish you you dislocated your leg, jumping here ...”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгел</a> (2474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄγγελος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ángelos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ángel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгела</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгелы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгелов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>angel</li>
<li>an innocent</li>
<li>dear, darling</li></ol>

<ol><li>English

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anglíjskij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йского</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>ан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гли́й<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ский</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">англійскій</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a✕~.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вший</a> (XVIII–XIX вв.) <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ния</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>а́нглийский</a>.

***аннулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аннулировать.html>аннули́ровать</a> (26390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аннулировать.html>аннули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">annulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to annul, to cancel, to nullify</li>
<li>to abrogate, to rescind, to repeal, to revoke, to abolish</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>ан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-аннул-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ир-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ансамбль.html>анса́мбль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ansámblʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ансамбль.html>анса́мбля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ансамбль.html>анса́мбли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ансамбль.html>анса́мблей</a></b>)
</p>

***антилопа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:антилопа.html>антило́па</a> (21768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антилопа.html>антило́па</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">antilópa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антилопа.html>антило́пы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антилопа.html>антило́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:антилопа.html>антило́п</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>antelope (any of several African mammals of the family Bovidae)</li></ol>
